	var shippingCountries = ['CA'];
	var billingCountries = ['CA','US'];
	var cookiesDisabledUrl = 'https://www.costco.ca/cookies-disabled.html';
	
	if (typeof checkCookieEnablement === "undefined") {
		function isCookieSupported() {
			var persist= true;
			do {
				var rand = Math.floor(Math.random()*100000000);
				var c= 'gCStest='+rand;
				document.cookie= persist? c+'; expires=Tue, 01-Jan-2030 00:00:00 GMT' : c;
				if (document.cookie.indexOf(c)!==-1) {
					document.cookie= c+'; expires=Sat, 01-Jan-2000 00:00:00 GMT';
					return persist;
				}
			} while (!(persist= !persist));
			return false;
		}
		
		function checkCookieEnablement() {
			if (!isCookieSupported() && window.location.href.indexOf('cookies-disabled') < 0) {
				window.location.replace(cookiesDisabledUrl);
			}
		};
	}
	
	checkCookieEnablement();

		<script>
		
		var initZoomViewer = function() {
			
			//returns zoom viewer size for the current window width
			function getViewerSize() {
				var width = $(window).width();
				if (width > 1000 || (width <= 667 && width > 382)) return zoomViewer.xl;
				if (width > 764) return zoomViewer.lg;
				return zoomViewer.xs;
			}
			
			//adds src attribute to script tag for the Rich Media zoom viewer library
			//and to img tag for the zoom viewer object to initiate injection by Rich Media
			function createViewer(viewerSize) {
				currentViewer = viewerSize;
				$viewerLib.attr('src', zoomViewer.libraryUrl + viewerSize);
				$viewerImg.attr('src', zoomViewer.viewerUrl + viewerSize.substr(2));
			}
			
			//changes size of viewer if current window size requires a different size
			function updateViewer() {
				var newViewerSize = getViewerSize();
				if (newViewerSize != currentViewer) {
					COSTCO.Global.logger('Window resized to new view. Updating zoomViewer');
					$viewerDiv.css('visibility', 'hidden');
					$initialImage.show();
					destroyThumbnailCarousel();
					RICHFX.load.fullReset();
					$viewerImg = $('#productImage');
					createViewer(newViewerSize);
					RICHFX.settings.init();
				}
				else if ($theViews.children().length) {
					adjustThumbnails();
				}
			}
			
			//adjusts thumbnail width and position of video overlay images
			function adjustThumbnails() {
				var thumbWidth = Math.floor($theViews.width() / 6);
				$theViews.find('img').css('width', thumbWidth);
				var $vidOverlay = $('img[id*=videoOverlay]');
				$vidOverlay.each(function() {
					$(this).parent().css('width', '');
					$(this).parent().css('height', '');
					$(this).css('left', $(this).siblings().position().left);
				});
			}
			
			//adds responsive properties to the zoom viewer
			function makeViewerResponsive() {
				COSTCO.Global.logger('richmedia.state.loaded - ZoomViewer injected. Adding responsive properties.');
				var $container = $('.RICHFXViewerContainer');
				$container.css('width', '');
				$container.css('height', '');
				$('#zoomViewer').find('img').addClass('img-responsive');
				if ($theViews.find('img').length) {
					$thumbnails.show();
					setupThumbnailCarousel();
				}
			}
			
			//creates thumbnail carousel
			function setupThumbnailCarousel(){
				if (currentSlide == 'undefined') {
					currentSlide = 0;
				}
				if (firstActiveSlide == 'undefined') {
					firstActiveSlide = 0;
				}
				var slides = $theViews.find('a').length;
				COSTCO.util.carousel($theViews,{
			        dots: false,
			        arrows: true,
			        slidesToShow: 5,
			        infinite: false,
			        slidesToScroll: 5,
			        autoplay: false,
			        draggable: true,
			        prevArrow: $('#viewsPrevArrow'),
			        nextArrow: $('#viewsNextArrow')
			    });
				$theViews.slick('slickGoTo', 5 * (Math.ceil(firstActiveSlide / 5)), true); //go to the set of 5 slides that were active
				$theViews.find('.selectedSlide').removeClass('selectedSlide');
				$theViews.find('.slick-slide:nth-child(' + (currentSlide + 1) + ')').addClass('selectedSlide');
				adjustThumbnails();
				if (slides > 5) {
					$prevArrow.addClass('slick-prev').css('visibility', 'visible');
					$nextArrow.addClass('slick-next').css('visibility', 'visible');
				}
				else {
					$prevArrow.css('visibility', 'hidden');
					$nextArrow.css('visibility', 'hidden');
				}
				$theViews.unbind('afterChange').on('afterChange', function() {
					firstActiveSlide = $('.slick-active').first().attr('data-slick-index');
				})
			}
			
			//destroys thumbnail carousel
			function destroyThumbnailCarousel() {
				$theViews.slick('destroy');
				$theViews.find('a[tabindex]').remove();
				$prevArrow.css('visibility', 'hidden');
				$prevArrow.css('visibility', 'hidden');
			}
			
			function loadVideoData() {
				COSTCO.Global.logger('External Video Detected. Loading Liveclicker.');
				$('#liveClickerCss').attr('href', zoomViewer.videoCssUrl);
				$.cachedScript(zoomViewer.videoJqueryUrl).done(function() {
					$.cachedScript(zoomViewer.videoJsUrl);
				});
				document.addEventListener('RichMedia.ExternalVideo.Show', function() {
					$('#zoomInstruction').hide();
				});
				document.addEventListener('RichMedia.ExternalVideo.Hide', function() {
					$('#zoomInstruction').show();
				})
			}
			
			var $viewerDiv = $('#zoomViewer');
			var $viewerLib = $('#productImageLibrary');
			var $viewerImg = $('#productImage');
			var $thumbnails = $('#thumbnails');
			var $theViews = $('#theViews');
			var $theSwatches = $('#theSwatches');
			var $initialImage = $('#initialProductImage');
			var $prevArrow = $('#viewsPrevArrow');
			var $nextArrow = $('#viewsNextArrow')
			var viewerSize = getViewerSize();
			var currentViewer = viewerSize;
			var currentSlide = 0;
			var firstActiveSlide = 0;
			
			document.addEventListener('richmedia.state.loaded', function() {
				makeViewerResponsive();
				if ($('.swatchDropdown').length > 0) { //select initial swatch
					try{
						var swatch = $('.swatchDropdown').find('option[data-swatch]').first().data('swatch');
						COSTCO.CMath.triggerSwatchDropDownSelection(swatch);
					}catch(e){
						console.log('error on loading inventoried swatch - default to first available');
						$theSwatches.find('img').first().click();
					}
				}
				$initialImage.hide();
				$viewerDiv.css('visibility', 'visible');
				var $externalVideo = $theViews.find('img[id*=External]');
				if (typeof lc == 'undefined' && $externalVideo.length > 0) { //only load liveclicker files once
					loadVideoData();
				}
			});
			document.addEventListener('richmedia.view.changed', function() {
				var $selected = $('.RICHFXColorChangeViewSelected');
				destroyThumbnailCarousel();
				currentSlide = $selected.parent().index();
				setupThumbnailCarousel();
			});
			document.addEventListener('richmedia.swatch.changed', function() {
				if ($theViews.hasClass('slick-initialized')) {
					destroyThumbnailCarousel();
					currentSlide = 0;
					firstActiveSlide = 0;
					setupThumbnailCarousel();
				}
			});
			createViewer(viewerSize);
			
			//modify viewer size on window resize
			$(window).resize(COSTCO.util.debounce(updateViewer, 250));
			
		}
		
		initZoomViewer();
		
		
</script>
		
		<div id="product-details" class="col-xs-12 col-sm-12 col-md-6 col-xl-5 pull-right">
			<div class="row visible-xl">
				<div class="col-xs-12"> 
					<div class="product-h1-container visible-xl-block">
					</div>
					
						<div id="details-bazaar-voice" class="bazaar-voice">
						</div>
					
						<p class='item-number'>Item #<span data-sku="483778" itemprop="sku">483778</span></p>
						
				</div>
			</div>
			<!-- Math table  -->
<div class="row form-group">
	<div class="col-xs-12 col-sm-12 col-xl-9">
	
<div id="math-table">
	<div id="breakdown" class="hide row no-gutter">

<script type="text/javascript">

$( document ).ready(function() {
	if ($.cookie("rrDisabledPref") != 1) {
		console.log( "Document loaded. Firing HL Ad Request.." );
	
		if( $('#hl_1') != null) {
			var hashedUserId = $.cookie('hashedUserId');
			if (typeof(hashedUserId) == 'undefined' || hashedUserId == '' || hashedUserId == '""')
			{
				hashedUserId = null;
			};
		try {
		
		} catch (e) {
			console.error(e)
		}
		}
		
		
			try {
			
			var hlPricingHandler = function hlPricing(){
			
			 HLLibrary.newRequest()
		     .setTaxonomy("31838")
		     .setModule("ProductPageWeb2")
		     .setProperty("cUserId", hashedUserId)
		     .setProperty("hlPageType", "P")
		     .setProperty("parentsku", "100284782")
		     .setProperty("broadmatchtype", "3")
		     .setProperty("required_filters", "parentsku")
		     .submit("hl_1");
			
			}
			
			var hlHandler = function loadHLProductDetails(){
			
				 var isMember = COSTCO.util.getMemberCookie().costcoMember == true;
				 var mosItem = false && false;
				 var mapItem = false && !false;
				 var priceIsDisplayed = (!mosItem && !mapItem) || (mosItem && isMember) || (mapItem && isMember);
			     var hlUpdate = HLLibrary.newUpdate()
			     .setProperty("cUserId", hashedUserId)
			     .setProperty("hlPageType", "P")
			     .setProperty("parentsku", "100284782")
			     .setProperty("sku", "483778")
			     .setProperty("inStock", "1");
			     if (priceIsDisplayed) {
			     	hlUpdate.setProperty("price", process("MjkuOTk="))
			     	.setProperty("regularPrice", process("MjkuOTk="));
			     }
			     hlUpdate.submit();
		     
		     };
		     
		    $(window).load(function(){
		    	hlHandler();
		    });
		     
	     	var hlVisibilityHandler = COSTCO.util.onVisibilityChange($('#hl_1'), function() {
			
				$(window).unbind('scroll.hlHandler');
				
				console.log('HL Div in view and Firing Handler');
				
				hlPricingHandler();
			
			});

			//jQuery
			$(window).on('load scroll.hlHandler', hlVisibilityHandler); 
		     
	     } catch (e) {
	     	console.error(e)
	     }
		
	}
	else {
		console.log( "Document loaded. Product Recommendations Turned off" );
	}
});
</script>

	getDataUrl : "/AjaxMembershipMetaDataView?langId=-24&storeId=10302&catalogId=11201",
	payload : "",
	resultCode: "",
	funktions : new Array(),
	getDrawFunctions: function(){
		var widgets = $("div[data-membership-widget-draw-function]");
		for (var i = 0; i < widgets.length; ++i) {
			var funktion = $(widgets[i]).data('membership-widget-draw-function');	
    		MembershipMetaData.funktions.push(funktion);
    		
		}
	},
	processAjaxReturn:	function(data){
		COSTCO.util.LoginTimeout.updateActivity();
		
		// if resultCode is a failure message code, then payLoadData will not be fetched
		// which shall show an error message staying in edit mode of widget
		
		if(data != undefined){
		
			MembershipMetaData.payload = data;
			for (var i = 0; i < MembershipMetaData.funktions.length; ++i) {
  				var namespaces = MembershipMetaData.funktions[i].split(".");
  				var func = namespaces.pop();

				var regExp = /\(([^)]+)\)/; //get stuff from ()
				var matches = regExp.exec(func);
				if(matches==null){
					window[namespaces][func]();
				}
				else {
					var func1 = func.slice(0, func.indexOf("("));
					var param1 = matches[1]!=null?matches[1]:"";
					param1 = param1.replace(/\"/g, "").replace(/\'/g, "");

	  				try {
	 					window[namespaces][func1](param1);
	  				} catch(err){
					  console.log("Error in Calling Draw Widget" +namespaces+ ": " +err);
					}
				}
			}
			
			if (MembershipMetaData.payload.errorMessages.length > 0){
				for (var i = 0; i < MembershipMetaData.payload.errorMessages.length; ++i) {
					$('#crmMetaDataGlobalError').html(MembershipMetaData.payload.errorMessages[i]);
				}
				$('#crmMetaDataGlobalError').show();
				$('html, body').animate({ scrollTop: $('#crmMetaDataGlobalError') });
			}else{
				$('#crmMetaDataGlobalError').hide();
			}
			
			COSTCO.util.updateCappJson();
			COSTCO.util.processCappLogic();
		}
	},
	ajaxHandler : function(url, payload){
		
		COSTCO.util.LoginTimeout.checkTimeout();
		
		var pseudo = (new Date()).getTime();
		$.ajax({
			type: 'POST',
			url: url+"&pseudo="+pseudo,
			dataType: 'json',
			data: payload,
			success: function(data) { 
				COSTCO.util.LoginTimeout.updateActivity();
				MembershipMetaData.processAjaxReturn(data);
				$(".r1_spinnerFirstLoad").hide();
			},
			timeout: wcs.ajaxTimeout,
			error: function(x, t, m) {
				COSTCO.util.LoginTimeout.updateActivity();
        		if(t==="timeout") {
        			
        		} else {
		    	    
        		}
    		}
		});
	},
	getHumanReadablePrefix : function(prefixCode){
		if (prefixCode == "0001"){
			return MembershipMetaData.PREFIX["0001"]
		}else if (prefixCode == "0002"){
			return MembershipMetaData.PREFIX["0002"]
		}else if (prefixCode == "0003"){
			return MembershipMetaData.PREFIX["0003"]
		}else if (prefixCode == "0004"){
			return MembershipMetaData.PREFIX["0004"]
		}else if (prefixCode == "Z005"){
			return MembershipMetaData.PREFIX["Z005"]
		}else if (prefixCode == "Z001"){
			return MembershipMetaData.PREFIX["Z001"]
		}
		return prefixCode;
	},
	getHumanReadableSuffix : function(suffixCode){
		if (suffixCode == "0001"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["0001"]
		}else if (suffixCode == "0002"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["0002"]
		}else if (suffixCode == "0003"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["0003"]
		}else if (suffixCode == "0004"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["0004"]
		}else if (suffixCode == "0005"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["0005"]
		}else if (suffixCode == "0006"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["0006"]
		}else if (suffixCode == "0007"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["0007"]
		}else if (suffixCode == "Z001"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["Z001"]
		}else if (suffixCode == "Z002"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["Z002"]
		}else if (suffixCode == "Z003"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["Z003"]
		}
		return suffixCode;
	},
	unProtectFields : function(jqSelector){
		var formFields = $(jqSelector).find("input[type='text']  ,select");
		
		for (var i = 0; i < formFields.length; ++i) {
			var protect = $(formFields[i]).data("membership-widget-protect-field");
			
			if (MembershipMetaData.FIELD_TYPE.READ_ONLY != protect){
				if( $(formFields[i]).is('input')){
					$(formFields[i]).attr('readonly', false);
					$(formFields[i]).css({border: "1px solid #dbdbdb"});
				}else{
					$(formFields[i]).attr('disabled', false);
				}
				if(MembershipMetaData.FIELD_TYPE.EDITABLE_REQUIRED == protect){
					//$(formFields[i]).rules('add', { required:true});
					
				}else if (MembershipMetaData.FIELD_TYPE.DO_NOT_DISPLAY == protect){
					$(formFields[i]).val('');
					if( $(formFields[i]).is('input')){
						$(formFields[i]).attr('readonly', true);
						$(formFields[i]).css({border: "none"});
					}else{
						$(formFields[i]).attr('disabled', true);			
					}
				}	
			}
		}
	},
	protectFields : function(jqSelector){
		var formFields = $(jqSelector).find("input[type='text']  ,select");
		for (var i = 0; i < formFields.length; ++i) {
			if( $(formFields[i]).is('input')){
				$(formFields[i]).attr('readonly', true);
				$(formFields[i]).css({border: "none"});
			}else{
				$(formFields[i]).attr('disabled', true);			
			}
		}
	},
	protectDisplayFields : function(jqSelector){
		for (var i = 0; i < jqSelector.length; ++i) {
			var protection = $(jqSelector[i]).data('membership-widget-protect-field');	
    		if (MembershipMetaData.FIELD_TYPE.DO_NOT_DISPLAY == protection){
    			$(jqSelector[i]).hide();
    		}else{
    			$(jqSelector[i]).show();
    		}
		}
	},
	ajaxSend : function(){
		var spinner = '<div class="ui-widget-overlay ui-front r1_spinner" id="crmMetaDataGlobalSpinner"></div>'
		$("body").append( spinner );
	},
	ajaxComplete : function(){
		$('#crmMetaDataGlobalSpinner').remove();
	}
}

// Changing document.ready to window.onload, document.ready not workingin some pages for some reason
$(window).load(function(){
	
			if(typeof skipFooterMembershipMetaDataCall == 'undefined' || skipFooterMembershipMetaDataCall == false){
				var mosInfo = COSTCO.util.getMemberCookie();
				MembershipMetaData.getDataUrl = "https://" + location.hostname + "/AjaxCitiMembershipMetaDataView?langId=-24&storeId=10302&catalogId=11201";
				if($.cookie("capp_json") == null && mosInfo && mosInfo.signedIn == true && mosInfo.costcoMember == true){
					MembershipMetaData.ajaxHandler(MembershipMetaData.getDataUrl, null);
				}
			}
		
});
</script>

		MAX_ITEM_QUANTITY : 999

	var shippingCountries = ['CA'];
	var billingCountries = ['CA','US'];
	var cookiesDisabledUrl = 'https://www.costco.ca/cookies-disabled.html';
	
	if (typeof checkCookieEnablement === "undefined") {
		function isCookieSupported() {
			var persist= true;
			do {
				var rand = Math.floor(Math.random()*100000000);
				var c= 'gCStest='+rand;
				document.cookie= persist? c+'; expires=Tue, 01-Jan-2030 00:00:00 GMT' : c;
				if (document.cookie.indexOf(c)!==-1) {
					document.cookie= c+'; expires=Sat, 01-Jan-2000 00:00:00 GMT';
					return persist;
				}
			} while (!(persist= !persist));
			return false;
		}
		
		function checkCookieEnablement() {
			if (!isCookieSupported() && window.location.href.indexOf('cookies-disabled') < 0) {
				window.location.replace(cookiesDisabledUrl);
			}
		};
	}
	
	checkCookieEnablement();

		<script>
		
		var initZoomViewer = function() {
			
			//returns zoom viewer size for the current window width
			function getViewerSize() {
				var width = $(window).width();
				if (width > 1000 || (width <= 667 && width > 382)) return zoomViewer.xl;
				if (width > 764) return zoomViewer.lg;
				return zoomViewer.xs;
			}
			
			//adds src attribute to script tag for the Rich Media zoom viewer library
			//and to img tag for the zoom viewer object to initiate injection by Rich Media
			function createViewer(viewerSize) {
				currentViewer = viewerSize;
				$viewerLib.attr('src', zoomViewer.libraryUrl + viewerSize);
				$viewerImg.attr('src', zoomViewer.viewerUrl + viewerSize.substr(2));
			}
			
			//changes size of viewer if current window size requires a different size
			function updateViewer() {
				var newViewerSize = getViewerSize();
				if (newViewerSize != currentViewer) {
					COSTCO.Global.logger('Window resized to new view. Updating zoomViewer');
					$viewerDiv.css('visibility', 'hidden');
					$initialImage.show();
					destroyThumbnailCarousel();
					RICHFX.load.fullReset();
					$viewerImg = $('#productImage');
					createViewer(newViewerSize);
					RICHFX.settings.init();
				}
				else if ($theViews.children().length) {
					adjustThumbnails();
				}
			}
			
			//adjusts thumbnail width and position of video overlay images
			function adjustThumbnails() {
				var thumbWidth = Math.floor($theViews.width() / 6);
				$theViews.find('img').css('width', thumbWidth);
				var $vidOverlay = $('img[id*=videoOverlay]');
				$vidOverlay.each(function() {
					$(this).parent().css('width', '');
					$(this).parent().css('height', '');
					$(this).css('left', $(this).siblings().position().left);
				});
			}
			
			//adds responsive properties to the zoom viewer
			function makeViewerResponsive() {
				COSTCO.Global.logger('richmedia.state.loaded - ZoomViewer injected. Adding responsive properties.');
				var $container = $('.RICHFXViewerContainer');
				$container.css('width', '');
				$container.css('height', '');
				$('#zoomViewer').find('img').addClass('img-responsive');
				if ($theViews.find('img').length) {
					$thumbnails.show();
					setupThumbnailCarousel();
				}
			}
			
			//creates thumbnail carousel
			function setupThumbnailCarousel(){
				if (currentSlide == 'undefined') {
					currentSlide = 0;
				}
				if (firstActiveSlide == 'undefined') {
					firstActiveSlide = 0;
				}
				var slides = $theViews.find('a').length;
				COSTCO.util.carousel($theViews,{
			        dots: false,
			        arrows: true,
			        slidesToShow: 5,
			        infinite: false,
			        slidesToScroll: 5,
			        autoplay: false,
			        draggable: true,
			        prevArrow: $('#viewsPrevArrow'),
			        nextArrow: $('#viewsNextArrow')
			    });
				$theViews.slick('slickGoTo', 5 * (Math.ceil(firstActiveSlide / 5)), true); //go to the set of 5 slides that were active
				$theViews.find('.selectedSlide').removeClass('selectedSlide');
				$theViews.find('.slick-slide:nth-child(' + (currentSlide + 1) + ')').addClass('selectedSlide');
				adjustThumbnails();
				if (slides > 5) {
					$prevArrow.addClass('slick-prev').css('visibility', 'visible');
					$nextArrow.addClass('slick-next').css('visibility', 'visible');
				}
				else {
					$prevArrow.css('visibility', 'hidden');
					$nextArrow.css('visibility', 'hidden');
				}
				$theViews.unbind('afterChange').on('afterChange', function() {
					firstActiveSlide = $('.slick-active').first().attr('data-slick-index');
				})
			}
			
			//destroys thumbnail carousel
			function destroyThumbnailCarousel() {
				$theViews.slick('destroy');
				$theViews.find('a[tabindex]').remove();
				$prevArrow.css('visibility', 'hidden');
				$prevArrow.css('visibility', 'hidden');
			}
			
			function loadVideoData() {
				COSTCO.Global.logger('External Video Detected. Loading Liveclicker.');
				$('#liveClickerCss').attr('href', zoomViewer.videoCssUrl);
				$.cachedScript(zoomViewer.videoJqueryUrl).done(function() {
					$.cachedScript(zoomViewer.videoJsUrl);
				});
				document.addEventListener('RichMedia.ExternalVideo.Show', function() {
					$('#zoomInstruction').hide();
				});
				document.addEventListener('RichMedia.ExternalVideo.Hide', function() {
					$('#zoomInstruction').show();
				})
			}
			
			var $viewerDiv = $('#zoomViewer');
			var $viewerLib = $('#productImageLibrary');
			var $viewerImg = $('#productImage');
			var $thumbnails = $('#thumbnails');
			var $theViews = $('#theViews');
			var $theSwatches = $('#theSwatches');
			var $initialImage = $('#initialProductImage');
			var $prevArrow = $('#viewsPrevArrow');
			var $nextArrow = $('#viewsNextArrow')
			var viewerSize = getViewerSize();
			var currentViewer = viewerSize;
			var currentSlide = 0;
			var firstActiveSlide = 0;
			
			document.addEventListener('richmedia.state.loaded', function() {
				makeViewerResponsive();
				if ($('.swatchDropdown').length > 0) { //select initial swatch
					try{
						var swatch = $('.swatchDropdown').find('option[data-swatch]').first().data('swatch');
						COSTCO.CMath.triggerSwatchDropDownSelection(swatch);
					}catch(e){
						console.log('error on loading inventoried swatch - default to first available');
						$theSwatches.find('img').first().click();
					}
				}
				$initialImage.hide();
				$viewerDiv.css('visibility', 'visible');
				var $externalVideo = $theViews.find('img[id*=External]');
				if (typeof lc == 'undefined' && $externalVideo.length > 0) { //only load liveclicker files once
					loadVideoData();
				}
			});
			document.addEventListener('richmedia.view.changed', function() {
				var $selected = $('.RICHFXColorChangeViewSelected');
				destroyThumbnailCarousel();
				currentSlide = $selected.parent().index();
				setupThumbnailCarousel();
			});
			document.addEventListener('richmedia.swatch.changed', function() {
				if ($theViews.hasClass('slick-initialized')) {
					destroyThumbnailCarousel();
					currentSlide = 0;
					firstActiveSlide = 0;
					setupThumbnailCarousel();
				}
			});
			createViewer(viewerSize);
			
			//modify viewer size on window resize
			$(window).resize(COSTCO.util.debounce(updateViewer, 250));
			
		}
		
		initZoomViewer();
		
		
</script>
		
		<div id="product-details" class="col-xs-12 col-sm-12 col-md-6 col-xl-5 pull-right">
			<div class="row visible-xl">
				<div class="col-xs-12"> 
					<div class="product-h1-container visible-xl-block">
					</div>
					
						<div id="details-bazaar-voice" class="bazaar-voice">
						</div>
					
						<p class='item-number'>Item #<span data-sku="483778" itemprop="sku">483778</span></p>
						
				</div>
			</div>
			<!-- Math table  -->
<div class="row form-group">
	<div class="col-xs-12 col-sm-12 col-xl-9">
	
<div id="math-table">
	<div id="breakdown" class="hide row no-gutter">

						<span class="op-value">MjkuOTk=</span>

<script type="text/javascript">

$( document ).ready(function() {
	if ($.cookie("rrDisabledPref") != 1) {
		console.log( "Document loaded. Firing HL Ad Request.." );
	
		if( $('#hl_1') != null) {
			var hashedUserId = $.cookie('hashedUserId');
			if (typeof(hashedUserId) == 'undefined' || hashedUserId == '' || hashedUserId == '""')
			{
				hashedUserId = null;
			};
		try {
		
		} catch (e) {
			console.error(e)
		}
		}
		
		
			try {
			
			var hlPricingHandler = function hlPricing(){
			
			 HLLibrary.newRequest()
		     .setTaxonomy("31838")
		     .setModule("ProductPageWeb2")
		     .setProperty("cUserId", hashedUserId)
		     .setProperty("hlPageType", "P")
		     .setProperty("parentsku", "100284782")
		     .setProperty("broadmatchtype", "3")
		     .setProperty("required_filters", "parentsku")
		     .submit("hl_1");
			
			}
			
			var hlHandler = function loadHLProductDetails(){
			
				 var isMember = COSTCO.util.getMemberCookie().costcoMember == true;
				 var mosItem = false && false;
				 var mapItem = false && !false;
				 var priceIsDisplayed = (!mosItem && !mapItem) || (mosItem && isMember) || (mapItem && isMember);
			     var hlUpdate = HLLibrary.newUpdate()
			     .setProperty("cUserId", hashedUserId)
			     .setProperty("hlPageType", "P")
			     .setProperty("parentsku", "100284782")
			     .setProperty("sku", "483778")
			     .setProperty("inStock", "1");
			     if (priceIsDisplayed) {
			     	hlUpdate.setProperty("price", process("MjkuOTk="))
			     	.setProperty("regularPrice", process("MjkuOTk="));
			     }
			     hlUpdate.submit();
		     
		     };
		     
		    $(window).load(function(){
		    	hlHandler();
		    });
		     
	     	var hlVisibilityHandler = COSTCO.util.onVisibilityChange($('#hl_1'), function() {
			
				$(window).unbind('scroll.hlHandler');
				
				console.log('HL Div in view and Firing Handler');
				
				hlPricingHandler();
			
			});

			//jQuery
			$(window).on('load scroll.hlHandler', hlVisibilityHandler); 
		     
	     } catch (e) {
	     	console.error(e)
	     }
		
	}
	else {
		console.log( "Document loaded. Product Recommendations Turned off" );
	}
});
</script>

	SUFFIX : {

		"0007" : "M.D.",
		"Z003" : "II",
		"Z001" : "R.N.",
		"Z002": "DDS"
	},
	getDataUrl : "/AjaxMembershipMetaDataView?langId=-24&storeId=10302&catalogId=11201",
	payload : "",
	resultCode: "",
	funktions : new Array(),
	getDrawFunctions: function(){
		var widgets = $("div[data-membership-widget-draw-function]");
		for (var i = 0; i < widgets.length; ++i) {
			var funktion = $(widgets[i]).data('membership-widget-draw-function');	
    		MembershipMetaData.funktions.push(funktion);
    		
		}
	},
	processAjaxReturn:	function(data){
		COSTCO.util.LoginTimeout.updateActivity();
		
		// if resultCode is a failure message code, then payLoadData will not be fetched
		// which shall show an error message staying in edit mode of widget
		
		if(data != undefined){
		
			MembershipMetaData.payload = data;
			for (var i = 0; i < MembershipMetaData.funktions.length; ++i) {
  				var namespaces = MembershipMetaData.funktions[i].split(".");
  				var func = namespaces.pop();

				var regExp = /\(([^)]+)\)/; //get stuff from ()
				var matches = regExp.exec(func);
				if(matches==null){
					window[namespaces][func]();
				}
				else {
					var func1 = func.slice(0, func.indexOf("("));
					var param1 = matches[1]!=null?matches[1]:"";
					param1 = param1.replace(/\"/g, "").replace(/\'/g, "");

	  				try {
	 					window[namespaces][func1](param1);
	  				} catch(err){
					  console.log("Error in Calling Draw Widget" +namespaces+ ": " +err);
					}
				}
			}
			
			if (MembershipMetaData.payload.errorMessages.length > 0){
				for (var i = 0; i < MembershipMetaData.payload.errorMessages.length; ++i) {
					$('#crmMetaDataGlobalError').html(MembershipMetaData.payload.errorMessages[i]);
				}
				$('#crmMetaDataGlobalError').show();
				$('html, body').animate({ scrollTop: $('#crmMetaDataGlobalError') });
			}else{
				$('#crmMetaDataGlobalError').hide();
			}
			
			COSTCO.util.updateCappJson();
			COSTCO.util.processCappLogic();
		}
	},
	ajaxHandler : function(url, payload){
		
		COSTCO.util.LoginTimeout.checkTimeout();
		
		var pseudo = (new Date()).getTime();
		$.ajax({
			type: 'POST',
			url: url+"&pseudo="+pseudo,
			dataType: 'json',
			data: payload,
			success: function(data) { 
				COSTCO.util.LoginTimeout.updateActivity();
				MembershipMetaData.processAjaxReturn(data);
				$(".r1_spinnerFirstLoad").hide();
			},
			timeout: wcs.ajaxTimeout,
			error: function(x, t, m) {
				COSTCO.util.LoginTimeout.updateActivity();
        		if(t==="timeout") {
        			
        		} else {
		    	    
        		}
    		}
		});
	},
	getHumanReadablePrefix : function(prefixCode){
		if (prefixCode == "0001"){
			return MembershipMetaData.PREFIX["0001"]
		}else if (prefixCode == "0002"){
			return MembershipMetaData.PREFIX["0002"]
		}else if (prefixCode == "0003"){
			return MembershipMetaData.PREFIX["0003"]
		}else if (prefixCode == "0004"){
			return MembershipMetaData.PREFIX["0004"]
		}else if (prefixCode == "Z005"){
			return MembershipMetaData.PREFIX["Z005"]
		}else if (prefixCode == "Z001"){
			return MembershipMetaData.PREFIX["Z001"]
		}
		return prefixCode;
	},
	getHumanReadableSuffix : function(suffixCode){
		if (suffixCode == "0001"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["0001"]
		}else if (suffixCode == "0002"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["0002"]
		}else if (suffixCode == "0003"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["0003"]
		}else if (suffixCode == "0004"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["0004"]
		}else if (suffixCode == "0005"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["0005"]
		}else if (suffixCode == "0006"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["0006"]
		}else if (suffixCode == "0007"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["0007"]
		}else if (suffixCode == "Z001"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["Z001"]
		}else if (suffixCode == "Z002"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["Z002"]
		}else if (suffixCode == "Z003"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["Z003"]
		}
		return suffixCode;
	},
	unProtectFields : function(jqSelector){
		var formFields = $(jqSelector).find("input[type='text']  ,select");
		
		for (var i = 0; i < formFields.length; ++i) {
			var protect = $(formFields[i]).data("membership-widget-protect-field");
			
			if (MembershipMetaData.FIELD_TYPE.READ_ONLY != protect){
				if( $(formFields[i]).is('input')){
					$(formFields[i]).attr('readonly', false);
					$(formFields[i]).css({border: "1px solid #dbdbdb"});
				}else{
					$(formFields[i]).attr('disabled', false);
				}
				if(MembershipMetaData.FIELD_TYPE.EDITABLE_REQUIRED == protect){
					//$(formFields[i]).rules('add', { required:true});
					
				}else if (MembershipMetaData.FIELD_TYPE.DO_NOT_DISPLAY == protect){
					$(formFields[i]).val('');
					if( $(formFields[i]).is('input')){
						$(formFields[i]).attr('readonly', true);
						$(formFields[i]).css({border: "none"});
					}else{
						$(formFields[i]).attr('disabled', true);			
					}
				}	
			}
		}
	},
	protectFields : function(jqSelector){
		var formFields = $(jqSelector).find("input[type='text']  ,select");
		for (var i = 0; i < formFields.length; ++i) {
			if( $(formFields[i]).is('input')){
				$(formFields[i]).attr('readonly', true);
				$(formFields[i]).css({border: "none"});
			}else{
				$(formFields[i]).attr('disabled', true);			
			}
		}
	},
	protectDisplayFields : function(jqSelector){
		for (var i = 0; i < jqSelector.length; ++i) {
			var protection = $(jqSelector[i]).data('membership-widget-protect-field');	
    		if (MembershipMetaData.FIELD_TYPE.DO_NOT_DISPLAY == protection){
    			$(jqSelector[i]).hide();
    		}else{
    			$(jqSelector[i]).show();
    		}
		}
	},
	ajaxSend : function(){
		var spinner = '<div class="ui-widget-overlay ui-front r1_spinner" id="crmMetaDataGlobalSpinner"></div>'
		$("body").append( spinner );
	},
	ajaxComplete : function(){
		$('#crmMetaDataGlobalSpinner').remove();
	}
}

// Changing document.ready to window.onload, document.ready not workingin some pages for some reason
$(window).load(function(){
	
			if(typeof skipFooterMembershipMetaDataCall == 'undefined' || skipFooterMembershipMetaDataCall == false){
				var mosInfo = COSTCO.util.getMemberCookie();
				MembershipMetaData.getDataUrl = "https://" + location.hostname + "/AjaxCitiMembershipMetaDataView?langId=-24&storeId=10302&catalogId=11201";
				if($.cookie("capp_json") == null && mosInfo && mosInfo.signedIn == true && mosInfo.costcoMember == true){
					MembershipMetaData.ajaxHandler(MembershipMetaData.getDataUrl, null);
				}
			}
		
});
</script>

			<span class="bold">What is a Flexible Spending Account (FSA)?</span><br>A FSA (Flexible Spending Account) allows use of the funds an individual has designated to be set aside pre-tax for medical expenses, typically with their employer, when selecting healthcare programs during the previous year.
		</p>

	var shippingCountries = ['CA'];
	var billingCountries = ['CA','US'];
	var cookiesDisabledUrl = 'https://www.costco.ca/cookies-disabled.html';
	
	if (typeof checkCookieEnablement === "undefined") {
		function isCookieSupported() {
			var persist= true;
			do {
				var rand = Math.floor(Math.random()*100000000);
				var c= 'gCStest='+rand;
				document.cookie= persist? c+'; expires=Tue, 01-Jan-2030 00:00:00 GMT' : c;
				if (document.cookie.indexOf(c)!==-1) {
					document.cookie= c+'; expires=Sat, 01-Jan-2000 00:00:00 GMT';
					return persist;
				}
			} while (!(persist= !persist));
			return false;
		}
		
		function checkCookieEnablement() {
			if (!isCookieSupported() && window.location.href.indexOf('cookies-disabled') < 0) {
				window.location.replace(cookiesDisabledUrl);
			}
		};
	}
	
	checkCookieEnablement();

		<script>
		
		var initZoomViewer = function() {
			
			//returns zoom viewer size for the current window width
			function getViewerSize() {
				var width = $(window).width();
				if (width > 1000 || (width <= 667 && width > 382)) return zoomViewer.xl;
				if (width > 764) return zoomViewer.lg;
				return zoomViewer.xs;
			}
			
			//adds src attribute to script tag for the Rich Media zoom viewer library
			//and to img tag for the zoom viewer object to initiate injection by Rich Media
			function createViewer(viewerSize) {
				currentViewer = viewerSize;
				$viewerLib.attr('src', zoomViewer.libraryUrl + viewerSize);
				$viewerImg.attr('src', zoomViewer.viewerUrl + viewerSize.substr(2));
			}
			
			//changes size of viewer if current window size requires a different size
			function updateViewer() {
				var newViewerSize = getViewerSize();
				if (newViewerSize != currentViewer) {
					COSTCO.Global.logger('Window resized to new view. Updating zoomViewer');
					$viewerDiv.css('visibility', 'hidden');
					$initialImage.show();
					destroyThumbnailCarousel();
					RICHFX.load.fullReset();
					$viewerImg = $('#productImage');
					createViewer(newViewerSize);
					RICHFX.settings.init();
				}
				else if ($theViews.children().length) {
					adjustThumbnails();
				}
			}
			
			//adjusts thumbnail width and position of video overlay images
			function adjustThumbnails() {
				var thumbWidth = Math.floor($theViews.width() / 6);
				$theViews.find('img').css('width', thumbWidth);
				var $vidOverlay = $('img[id*=videoOverlay]');
				$vidOverlay.each(function() {
					$(this).parent().css('width', '');
					$(this).parent().css('height', '');
					$(this).css('left', $(this).siblings().position().left);
				});
			}
			
			//adds responsive properties to the zoom viewer
			function makeViewerResponsive() {
				COSTCO.Global.logger('richmedia.state.loaded - ZoomViewer injected. Adding responsive properties.');
				var $container = $('.RICHFXViewerContainer');
				$container.css('width', '');
				$container.css('height', '');
				$('#zoomViewer').find('img').addClass('img-responsive');
				if ($theViews.find('img').length) {
					$thumbnails.show();
					setupThumbnailCarousel();
				}
			}
			
			//creates thumbnail carousel
			function setupThumbnailCarousel(){
				if (currentSlide == 'undefined') {
					currentSlide = 0;
				}
				if (firstActiveSlide == 'undefined') {
					firstActiveSlide = 0;
				}
				var slides = $theViews.find('a').length;
				COSTCO.util.carousel($theViews,{
			        dots: false,
			        arrows: true,
			        slidesToShow: 5,
			        infinite: false,
			        slidesToScroll: 5,
			        autoplay: false,
			        draggable: true,
			        prevArrow: $('#viewsPrevArrow'),
			        nextArrow: $('#viewsNextArrow')
			    });
				$theViews.slick('slickGoTo', 5 * (Math.ceil(firstActiveSlide / 5)), true); //go to the set of 5 slides that were active
				$theViews.find('.selectedSlide').removeClass('selectedSlide');
				$theViews.find('.slick-slide:nth-child(' + (currentSlide + 1) + ')').addClass('selectedSlide');
				adjustThumbnails();
				if (slides > 5) {
					$prevArrow.addClass('slick-prev').css('visibility', 'visible');
					$nextArrow.addClass('slick-next').css('visibility', 'visible');
				}
				else {
					$prevArrow.css('visibility', 'hidden');
					$nextArrow.css('visibility', 'hidden');
				}
				$theViews.unbind('afterChange').on('afterChange', function() {
					firstActiveSlide = $('.slick-active').first().attr('data-slick-index');
				})
			}
			
			//destroys thumbnail carousel
			function destroyThumbnailCarousel() {
				$theViews.slick('destroy');
				$theViews.find('a[tabindex]').remove();
				$prevArrow.css('visibility', 'hidden');
				$prevArrow.css('visibility', 'hidden');
			}
			
			function loadVideoData() {
				COSTCO.Global.logger('External Video Detected. Loading Liveclicker.');
				$('#liveClickerCss').attr('href', zoomViewer.videoCssUrl);
				$.cachedScript(zoomViewer.videoJqueryUrl).done(function() {
					$.cachedScript(zoomViewer.videoJsUrl);
				});
				document.addEventListener('RichMedia.ExternalVideo.Show', function() {
					$('#zoomInstruction').hide();
				});
				document.addEventListener('RichMedia.ExternalVideo.Hide', function() {
					$('#zoomInstruction').show();
				})
			}
			
			var $viewerDiv = $('#zoomViewer');
			var $viewerLib = $('#productImageLibrary');
			var $viewerImg = $('#productImage');
			var $thumbnails = $('#thumbnails');
			var $theViews = $('#theViews');
			var $theSwatches = $('#theSwatches');
			var $initialImage = $('#initialProductImage');
			var $prevArrow = $('#viewsPrevArrow');
			var $nextArrow = $('#viewsNextArrow')
			var viewerSize = getViewerSize();
			var currentViewer = viewerSize;
			var currentSlide = 0;
			var firstActiveSlide = 0;
			
			document.addEventListener('richmedia.state.loaded', function() {
				makeViewerResponsive();
				if ($('.swatchDropdown').length > 0) { //select initial swatch
					try{
						var swatch = $('.swatchDropdown').find('option[data-swatch]').first().data('swatch');
						COSTCO.CMath.triggerSwatchDropDownSelection(swatch);
					}catch(e){
						console.log('error on loading inventoried swatch - default to first available');
						$theSwatches.find('img').first().click();
					}
				}
				$initialImage.hide();
				$viewerDiv.css('visibility', 'visible');
				var $externalVideo = $theViews.find('img[id*=External]');
				if (typeof lc == 'undefined' && $externalVideo.length > 0) { //only load liveclicker files once
					loadVideoData();
				}
			});
			document.addEventListener('richmedia.view.changed', function() {
				var $selected = $('.RICHFXColorChangeViewSelected');
				destroyThumbnailCarousel();
				currentSlide = $selected.parent().index();
				setupThumbnailCarousel();
			});
			document.addEventListener('richmedia.swatch.changed', function() {
				if ($theViews.hasClass('slick-initialized')) {
					destroyThumbnailCarousel();
					currentSlide = 0;
					firstActiveSlide = 0;
					setupThumbnailCarousel();
				}
			});
			createViewer(viewerSize);
			
			//modify viewer size on window resize
			$(window).resize(COSTCO.util.debounce(updateViewer, 250));
			
		}
		
		initZoomViewer();
		
		
</script>
		
		<div id="product-details" class="col-xs-12 col-sm-12 col-md-6 col-xl-5 pull-right">
			<div class="row visible-xl">
				<div class="col-xs-12"> 
					<div class="product-h1-container visible-xl-block">
					</div>
					
						<div id="details-bazaar-voice" class="bazaar-voice">
						</div>
					
						<p class='item-number'>Item #<span data-sku="483778" itemprop="sku">483778</span></p>
						
				</div>
			</div>
			<!-- Math table  -->
<div class="row form-group">
	<div class="col-xs-12 col-sm-12 col-xl-9">
	
<div id="math-table">
	<div id="breakdown" class="hide row no-gutter">
		
					
					<div class="online-price hide" data-opvalue="MjkuOTk=" data-catentry="880404" data-inv="IN_STOCK">
						<span class="op-label">Online Price</span>
						<span class="op-value">MjkuOTk=</span>

					</div>

<script type="text/javascript">

$( document ).ready(function() {
	if ($.cookie("rrDisabledPref") != 1) {
		console.log( "Document loaded. Firing HL Ad Request.." );
	
		if( $('#hl_1') != null) {
			var hashedUserId = $.cookie('hashedUserId');
			if (typeof(hashedUserId) == 'undefined' || hashedUserId == '' || hashedUserId == '""')
			{
				hashedUserId = null;
			};
		try {
		
		} catch (e) {
			console.error(e)
		}
		}
		
		
			try {
			
			var hlPricingHandler = function hlPricing(){
			
			 HLLibrary.newRequest()
		     .setTaxonomy("31838")
		     .setModule("ProductPageWeb2")
		     .setProperty("cUserId", hashedUserId)
		     .setProperty("hlPageType", "P")
		     .setProperty("parentsku", "100284782")
		     .setProperty("broadmatchtype", "3")
		     .setProperty("required_filters", "parentsku")
		     .submit("hl_1");
			
			}
			
			var hlHandler = function loadHLProductDetails(){
			
				 var isMember = COSTCO.util.getMemberCookie().costcoMember == true;
				 var mosItem = false && false;
				 var mapItem = false && !false;
				 var priceIsDisplayed = (!mosItem && !mapItem) || (mosItem && isMember) || (mapItem && isMember);
			     var hlUpdate = HLLibrary.newUpdate()
			     .setProperty("cUserId", hashedUserId)
			     .setProperty("hlPageType", "P")
			     .setProperty("parentsku", "100284782")
			     .setProperty("sku", "483778")
			     .setProperty("inStock", "1");
			     if (priceIsDisplayed) {
			     	hlUpdate.setProperty("price", process("MjkuOTk="))
			     	.setProperty("regularPrice", process("MjkuOTk="));
			     }
			     hlUpdate.submit();
		     
		     };
		     
		    $(window).load(function(){
		    	hlHandler();
		    });
		     
	     	var hlVisibilityHandler = COSTCO.util.onVisibilityChange($('#hl_1'), function() {
			
				$(window).unbind('scroll.hlHandler');
				
				console.log('HL Div in view and Firing Handler');
				
				hlPricingHandler();
			
			});

			//jQuery
			$(window).on('load scroll.hlHandler', hlVisibilityHandler); 
		     
	     } catch (e) {
	     	console.error(e)
	     }
		
	}
	else {
		console.log( "Document loaded. Product Recommendations Turned off" );
	}
});
</script>

	},
	SUFFIX : {

		"0004" : "IV",
		"0005": "Esq.",

		"0007" : "M.D.",
		"Z003" : "II",
		"Z001" : "R.N.",
		"Z002": "DDS"
	},
	getDataUrl : "/AjaxMembershipMetaDataView?langId=-24&storeId=10302&catalogId=11201",
	payload : "",
	resultCode: "",
	funktions : new Array(),
	getDrawFunctions: function(){
		var widgets = $("div[data-membership-widget-draw-function]");
		for (var i = 0; i < widgets.length; ++i) {
			var funktion = $(widgets[i]).data('membership-widget-draw-function');	
    		MembershipMetaData.funktions.push(funktion);
    		
		}
	},
	processAjaxReturn:	function(data){
		COSTCO.util.LoginTimeout.updateActivity();
		
		// if resultCode is a failure message code, then payLoadData will not be fetched
		// which shall show an error message staying in edit mode of widget
		
		if(data != undefined){
		
			MembershipMetaData.payload = data;
			for (var i = 0; i < MembershipMetaData.funktions.length; ++i) {
  				var namespaces = MembershipMetaData.funktions[i].split(".");
  				var func = namespaces.pop();

				var regExp = /\(([^)]+)\)/; //get stuff from ()
				var matches = regExp.exec(func);
				if(matches==null){
					window[namespaces][func]();
				}
				else {
					var func1 = func.slice(0, func.indexOf("("));
					var param1 = matches[1]!=null?matches[1]:"";
					param1 = param1.replace(/\"/g, "").replace(/\'/g, "");

	  				try {
	 					window[namespaces][func1](param1);
	  				} catch(err){
					  console.log("Error in Calling Draw Widget" +namespaces+ ": " +err);
					}
				}
			}
			
			if (MembershipMetaData.payload.errorMessages.length > 0){
				for (var i = 0; i < MembershipMetaData.payload.errorMessages.length; ++i) {
					$('#crmMetaDataGlobalError').html(MembershipMetaData.payload.errorMessages[i]);
				}
				$('#crmMetaDataGlobalError').show();
				$('html, body').animate({ scrollTop: $('#crmMetaDataGlobalError') });
			}else{
				$('#crmMetaDataGlobalError').hide();
			}
			
			COSTCO.util.updateCappJson();
			COSTCO.util.processCappLogic();
		}
	},
	ajaxHandler : function(url, payload){
		
		COSTCO.util.LoginTimeout.checkTimeout();
		
		var pseudo = (new Date()).getTime();
		$.ajax({
			type: 'POST',
			url: url+"&pseudo="+pseudo,
			dataType: 'json',
			data: payload,
			success: function(data) { 
				COSTCO.util.LoginTimeout.updateActivity();
				MembershipMetaData.processAjaxReturn(data);
				$(".r1_spinnerFirstLoad").hide();
			},
			timeout: wcs.ajaxTimeout,
			error: function(x, t, m) {
				COSTCO.util.LoginTimeout.updateActivity();
        		if(t==="timeout") {
        			
        		} else {
		    	    
        		}
    		}
		});
	},
	getHumanReadablePrefix : function(prefixCode){
		if (prefixCode == "0001"){
			return MembershipMetaData.PREFIX["0001"]
		}else if (prefixCode == "0002"){
			return MembershipMetaData.PREFIX["0002"]
		}else if (prefixCode == "0003"){
			return MembershipMetaData.PREFIX["0003"]
		}else if (prefixCode == "0004"){
			return MembershipMetaData.PREFIX["0004"]
		}else if (prefixCode == "Z005"){
			return MembershipMetaData.PREFIX["Z005"]
		}else if (prefixCode == "Z001"){
			return MembershipMetaData.PREFIX["Z001"]
		}
		return prefixCode;
	},
	getHumanReadableSuffix : function(suffixCode){
		if (suffixCode == "0001"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["0001"]
		}else if (suffixCode == "0002"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["0002"]
		}else if (suffixCode == "0003"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["0003"]
		}else if (suffixCode == "0004"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["0004"]
		}else if (suffixCode == "0005"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["0005"]
		}else if (suffixCode == "0006"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["0006"]
		}else if (suffixCode == "0007"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["0007"]
		}else if (suffixCode == "Z001"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["Z001"]
		}else if (suffixCode == "Z002"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["Z002"]
		}else if (suffixCode == "Z003"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["Z003"]
		}
		return suffixCode;
	},
	unProtectFields : function(jqSelector){
		var formFields = $(jqSelector).find("input[type='text']  ,select");
		
		for (var i = 0; i < formFields.length; ++i) {
			var protect = $(formFields[i]).data("membership-widget-protect-field");
			
			if (MembershipMetaData.FIELD_TYPE.READ_ONLY != protect){
				if( $(formFields[i]).is('input')){
					$(formFields[i]).attr('readonly', false);
					$(formFields[i]).css({border: "1px solid #dbdbdb"});
				}else{
					$(formFields[i]).attr('disabled', false);
				}
				if(MembershipMetaData.FIELD_TYPE.EDITABLE_REQUIRED == protect){
					//$(formFields[i]).rules('add', { required:true});
					
				}else if (MembershipMetaData.FIELD_TYPE.DO_NOT_DISPLAY == protect){
					$(formFields[i]).val('');
					if( $(formFields[i]).is('input')){
						$(formFields[i]).attr('readonly', true);
						$(formFields[i]).css({border: "none"});
					}else{
						$(formFields[i]).attr('disabled', true);			
					}
				}	
			}
		}
	},
	protectFields : function(jqSelector){
		var formFields = $(jqSelector).find("input[type='text']  ,select");
		for (var i = 0; i < formFields.length; ++i) {
			if( $(formFields[i]).is('input')){
				$(formFields[i]).attr('readonly', true);
				$(formFields[i]).css({border: "none"});
			}else{
				$(formFields[i]).attr('disabled', true);			
			}
		}
	},
	protectDisplayFields : function(jqSelector){
		for (var i = 0; i < jqSelector.length; ++i) {
			var protection = $(jqSelector[i]).data('membership-widget-protect-field');	
    		if (MembershipMetaData.FIELD_TYPE.DO_NOT_DISPLAY == protection){
    			$(jqSelector[i]).hide();
    		}else{
    			$(jqSelector[i]).show();
    		}
		}
	},
	ajaxSend : function(){
		var spinner = '<div class="ui-widget-overlay ui-front r1_spinner" id="crmMetaDataGlobalSpinner"></div>'
		$("body").append( spinner );
	},
	ajaxComplete : function(){
		$('#crmMetaDataGlobalSpinner').remove();
	}
}

// Changing document.ready to window.onload, document.ready not workingin some pages for some reason
$(window).load(function(){
	
			if(typeof skipFooterMembershipMetaDataCall == 'undefined' || skipFooterMembershipMetaDataCall == false){
				var mosInfo = COSTCO.util.getMemberCookie();
				MembershipMetaData.getDataUrl = "https://" + location.hostname + "/AjaxCitiMembershipMetaDataView?langId=-24&storeId=10302&catalogId=11201";
				if($.cookie("capp_json") == null && mosInfo && mosInfo.signedIn == true && mosInfo.costcoMember == true){
					MembershipMetaData.ajaxHandler(MembershipMetaData.getDataUrl, null);
				}
			}
		
});
</script>

		</p>
			<span class="fsa-link">FSA Eligible Item</span>
		<p>
			<span class="bold">What is a Flexible Spending Account (FSA)?</span><br>A FSA (Flexible Spending Account) allows use of the funds an individual has designated to be set aside pre-tax for medical expenses, typically with their employer, when selecting healthcare programs during the previous year.
		</p>
		<p>
			<span class="bold">What types of purchases are FSA eligible?</span><br>Over-the-counter medical supplies and equipment are considered reimbursable by an FSA account in 2011 and include the following categories:

		MAX_ITEM_QUANTITY : 999

	var shippingCountries = ['CA'];
	var billingCountries = ['CA','US'];
	var cookiesDisabledUrl = 'https://www.costco.ca/cookies-disabled.html';
	
	if (typeof checkCookieEnablement === "undefined") {
		function isCookieSupported() {
			var persist= true;
			do {
				var rand = Math.floor(Math.random()*100000000);
				var c= 'gCStest='+rand;
				document.cookie= persist? c+'; expires=Tue, 01-Jan-2030 00:00:00 GMT' : c;
				if (document.cookie.indexOf(c)!==-1) {
					document.cookie= c+'; expires=Sat, 01-Jan-2000 00:00:00 GMT';
					return persist;
				}
			} while (!(persist= !persist));
			return false;
		}
		
		function checkCookieEnablement() {
			if (!isCookieSupported() && window.location.href.indexOf('cookies-disabled') < 0) {
				window.location.replace(cookiesDisabledUrl);
			}
		};
	}
	
	checkCookieEnablement();

		<script>
		
		var initZoomViewer = function() {
			
			//returns zoom viewer size for the current window width
			function getViewerSize() {
				var width = $(window).width();
				if (width > 1000 || (width <= 667 && width > 382)) return zoomViewer.xl;
				if (width > 764) return zoomViewer.lg;
				return zoomViewer.xs;
			}
			
			//adds src attribute to script tag for the Rich Media zoom viewer library
			//and to img tag for the zoom viewer object to initiate injection by Rich Media
			function createViewer(viewerSize) {
				currentViewer = viewerSize;
				$viewerLib.attr('src', zoomViewer.libraryUrl + viewerSize);
				$viewerImg.attr('src', zoomViewer.viewerUrl + viewerSize.substr(2));
			}
			
			//changes size of viewer if current window size requires a different size
			function updateViewer() {
				var newViewerSize = getViewerSize();
				if (newViewerSize != currentViewer) {
					COSTCO.Global.logger('Window resized to new view. Updating zoomViewer');
					$viewerDiv.css('visibility', 'hidden');
					$initialImage.show();
					destroyThumbnailCarousel();
					RICHFX.load.fullReset();
					$viewerImg = $('#productImage');
					createViewer(newViewerSize);
					RICHFX.settings.init();
				}
				else if ($theViews.children().length) {
					adjustThumbnails();
				}
			}
			
			//adjusts thumbnail width and position of video overlay images
			function adjustThumbnails() {
				var thumbWidth = Math.floor($theViews.width() / 6);
				$theViews.find('img').css('width', thumbWidth);
				var $vidOverlay = $('img[id*=videoOverlay]');
				$vidOverlay.each(function() {
					$(this).parent().css('width', '');
					$(this).parent().css('height', '');
					$(this).css('left', $(this).siblings().position().left);
				});
			}
			
			//adds responsive properties to the zoom viewer
			function makeViewerResponsive() {
				COSTCO.Global.logger('richmedia.state.loaded - ZoomViewer injected. Adding responsive properties.');
				var $container = $('.RICHFXViewerContainer');
				$container.css('width', '');
				$container.css('height', '');
				$('#zoomViewer').find('img').addClass('img-responsive');
				if ($theViews.find('img').length) {
					$thumbnails.show();
					setupThumbnailCarousel();
				}
			}
			
			//creates thumbnail carousel
			function setupThumbnailCarousel(){
				if (currentSlide == 'undefined') {
					currentSlide = 0;
				}
				if (firstActiveSlide == 'undefined') {
					firstActiveSlide = 0;
				}
				var slides = $theViews.find('a').length;
				COSTCO.util.carousel($theViews,{
			        dots: false,
			        arrows: true,
			        slidesToShow: 5,
			        infinite: false,
			        slidesToScroll: 5,
			        autoplay: false,
			        draggable: true,
			        prevArrow: $('#viewsPrevArrow'),
			        nextArrow: $('#viewsNextArrow')
			    });
				$theViews.slick('slickGoTo', 5 * (Math.ceil(firstActiveSlide / 5)), true); //go to the set of 5 slides that were active
				$theViews.find('.selectedSlide').removeClass('selectedSlide');
				$theViews.find('.slick-slide:nth-child(' + (currentSlide + 1) + ')').addClass('selectedSlide');
				adjustThumbnails();
				if (slides > 5) {
					$prevArrow.addClass('slick-prev').css('visibility', 'visible');
					$nextArrow.addClass('slick-next').css('visibility', 'visible');
				}
				else {
					$prevArrow.css('visibility', 'hidden');
					$nextArrow.css('visibility', 'hidden');
				}
				$theViews.unbind('afterChange').on('afterChange', function() {
					firstActiveSlide = $('.slick-active').first().attr('data-slick-index');
				})
			}
			
			//destroys thumbnail carousel
			function destroyThumbnailCarousel() {
				$theViews.slick('destroy');
				$theViews.find('a[tabindex]').remove();
				$prevArrow.css('visibility', 'hidden');
				$prevArrow.css('visibility', 'hidden');
			}
			
			function loadVideoData() {
				COSTCO.Global.logger('External Video Detected. Loading Liveclicker.');
				$('#liveClickerCss').attr('href', zoomViewer.videoCssUrl);
				$.cachedScript(zoomViewer.videoJqueryUrl).done(function() {
					$.cachedScript(zoomViewer.videoJsUrl);
				});
				document.addEventListener('RichMedia.ExternalVideo.Show', function() {
					$('#zoomInstruction').hide();
				});
				document.addEventListener('RichMedia.ExternalVideo.Hide', function() {
					$('#zoomInstruction').show();
				})
			}
			
			var $viewerDiv = $('#zoomViewer');
			var $viewerLib = $('#productImageLibrary');
			var $viewerImg = $('#productImage');
			var $thumbnails = $('#thumbnails');
			var $theViews = $('#theViews');
			var $theSwatches = $('#theSwatches');
			var $initialImage = $('#initialProductImage');
			var $prevArrow = $('#viewsPrevArrow');
			var $nextArrow = $('#viewsNextArrow')
			var viewerSize = getViewerSize();
			var currentViewer = viewerSize;
			var currentSlide = 0;
			var firstActiveSlide = 0;
			
			document.addEventListener('richmedia.state.loaded', function() {
				makeViewerResponsive();
				if ($('.swatchDropdown').length > 0) { //select initial swatch
					try{
						var swatch = $('.swatchDropdown').find('option[data-swatch]').first().data('swatch');
						COSTCO.CMath.triggerSwatchDropDownSelection(swatch);
					}catch(e){
						console.log('error on loading inventoried swatch - default to first available');
						$theSwatches.find('img').first().click();
					}
				}
				$initialImage.hide();
				$viewerDiv.css('visibility', 'visible');
				var $externalVideo = $theViews.find('img[id*=External]');
				if (typeof lc == 'undefined' && $externalVideo.length > 0) { //only load liveclicker files once
					loadVideoData();
				}
			});
			document.addEventListener('richmedia.view.changed', function() {
				var $selected = $('.RICHFXColorChangeViewSelected');
				destroyThumbnailCarousel();
				currentSlide = $selected.parent().index();
				setupThumbnailCarousel();
			});
			document.addEventListener('richmedia.swatch.changed', function() {
				if ($theViews.hasClass('slick-initialized')) {
					destroyThumbnailCarousel();
					currentSlide = 0;
					firstActiveSlide = 0;
					setupThumbnailCarousel();
				}
			});
			createViewer(viewerSize);
			
			//modify viewer size on window resize
			$(window).resize(COSTCO.util.debounce(updateViewer, 250));
			
		}
		
		initZoomViewer();
		
		
</script>
		
		<div id="product-details" class="col-xs-12 col-sm-12 col-md-6 col-xl-5 pull-right">
			<div class="row visible-xl">
				<div class="col-xs-12"> 
					<div class="product-h1-container visible-xl-block">
					</div>
					
						<div id="details-bazaar-voice" class="bazaar-voice">
						</div>
					
						<p class='item-number'>Item #<span data-sku="483778" itemprop="sku">483778</span></p>
						
				</div>
			</div>
			<!-- Math table  -->
<div class="row form-group">
	<div class="col-xs-12 col-sm-12 col-xl-9">
	
<div id="math-table">
	<div id="breakdown" class="hide row no-gutter">

						<span class="op-value">MjkuOTk=</span>

<script type="text/javascript">

$( document ).ready(function() {
	if ($.cookie("rrDisabledPref") != 1) {
		console.log( "Document loaded. Firing HL Ad Request.." );
	
		if( $('#hl_1') != null) {
			var hashedUserId = $.cookie('hashedUserId');
			if (typeof(hashedUserId) == 'undefined' || hashedUserId == '' || hashedUserId == '""')
			{
				hashedUserId = null;
			};
		try {
		
		} catch (e) {
			console.error(e)
		}
		}
		
		
			try {
			
			var hlPricingHandler = function hlPricing(){
			
			 HLLibrary.newRequest()
		     .setTaxonomy("31838")
		     .setModule("ProductPageWeb2")
		     .setProperty("cUserId", hashedUserId)
		     .setProperty("hlPageType", "P")
		     .setProperty("parentsku", "100284782")
		     .setProperty("broadmatchtype", "3")
		     .setProperty("required_filters", "parentsku")
		     .submit("hl_1");
			
			}
			
			var hlHandler = function loadHLProductDetails(){
			
				 var isMember = COSTCO.util.getMemberCookie().costcoMember == true;
				 var mosItem = false && false;
				 var mapItem = false && !false;
				 var priceIsDisplayed = (!mosItem && !mapItem) || (mosItem && isMember) || (mapItem && isMember);
			     var hlUpdate = HLLibrary.newUpdate()
			     .setProperty("cUserId", hashedUserId)
			     .setProperty("hlPageType", "P")
			     .setProperty("parentsku", "100284782")
			     .setProperty("sku", "483778")
			     .setProperty("inStock", "1");
			     if (priceIsDisplayed) {
			     	hlUpdate.setProperty("price", process("MjkuOTk="))
			     	.setProperty("regularPrice", process("MjkuOTk="));
			     }
			     hlUpdate.submit();
		     
		     };
		     
		    $(window).load(function(){
		    	hlHandler();
		    });
		     
	     	var hlVisibilityHandler = COSTCO.util.onVisibilityChange($('#hl_1'), function() {
			
				$(window).unbind('scroll.hlHandler');
				
				console.log('HL Div in view and Firing Handler');
				
				hlPricingHandler();
			
			});

			//jQuery
			$(window).on('load scroll.hlHandler', hlVisibilityHandler); 
		     
	     } catch (e) {
	     	console.error(e)
	     }
		
	}
	else {
		console.log( "Document loaded. Product Recommendations Turned off" );
	}
});
</script>

	},
	RESULT_CODE:{

	PREFIX : {
		"0001" 	: "Mr.",
		"0002" : "Mrs.",
		"0003" 	: "Ms.",

		"Z001" : "Rev."
	},
	SUFFIX : {
		"0002" : "Jr.",
		"0001" : "Sr.",
		"0003": "III",
		"0004" : "IV",
		"0005": "Esq.",
		"0006": "PhD",
		"0007" : "M.D.",
		"Z003" : "II",
		"Z001" : "R.N.",
		"Z002": "DDS"
	},
	getDataUrl : "/AjaxMembershipMetaDataView?langId=-24&storeId=10302&catalogId=11201",
	payload : "",
	resultCode: "",
	funktions : new Array(),
	getDrawFunctions: function(){
		var widgets = $("div[data-membership-widget-draw-function]");
		for (var i = 0; i < widgets.length; ++i) {
			var funktion = $(widgets[i]).data('membership-widget-draw-function');	
    		MembershipMetaData.funktions.push(funktion);
    		
		}
	},
	processAjaxReturn:	function(data){
		COSTCO.util.LoginTimeout.updateActivity();
		
		// if resultCode is a failure message code, then payLoadData will not be fetched
		// which shall show an error message staying in edit mode of widget
		
		if(data != undefined){
		
			MembershipMetaData.payload = data;
			for (var i = 0; i < MembershipMetaData.funktions.length; ++i) {
  				var namespaces = MembershipMetaData.funktions[i].split(".");
  				var func = namespaces.pop();

				var regExp = /\(([^)]+)\)/; //get stuff from ()
				var matches = regExp.exec(func);
				if(matches==null){
					window[namespaces][func]();
				}
				else {
					var func1 = func.slice(0, func.indexOf("("));
					var param1 = matches[1]!=null?matches[1]:"";
					param1 = param1.replace(/\"/g, "").replace(/\'/g, "");

	  				try {
	 					window[namespaces][func1](param1);
	  				} catch(err){
					  console.log("Error in Calling Draw Widget" +namespaces+ ": " +err);
					}
				}
			}
			
			if (MembershipMetaData.payload.errorMessages.length > 0){
				for (var i = 0; i < MembershipMetaData.payload.errorMessages.length; ++i) {
					$('#crmMetaDataGlobalError').html(MembershipMetaData.payload.errorMessages[i]);
				}
				$('#crmMetaDataGlobalError').show();
				$('html, body').animate({ scrollTop: $('#crmMetaDataGlobalError') });
			}else{
				$('#crmMetaDataGlobalError').hide();
			}
			
			COSTCO.util.updateCappJson();
			COSTCO.util.processCappLogic();
		}
	},
	ajaxHandler : function(url, payload){
		
		COSTCO.util.LoginTimeout.checkTimeout();
		
		var pseudo = (new Date()).getTime();
		$.ajax({
			type: 'POST',
			url: url+"&pseudo="+pseudo,
			dataType: 'json',
			data: payload,
			success: function(data) { 
				COSTCO.util.LoginTimeout.updateActivity();
				MembershipMetaData.processAjaxReturn(data);
				$(".r1_spinnerFirstLoad").hide();
			},
			timeout: wcs.ajaxTimeout,
			error: function(x, t, m) {
				COSTCO.util.LoginTimeout.updateActivity();
        		if(t==="timeout") {
        			
        		} else {
		    	    
        		}
    		}
		});
	},
	getHumanReadablePrefix : function(prefixCode){
		if (prefixCode == "0001"){
			return MembershipMetaData.PREFIX["0001"]
		}else if (prefixCode == "0002"){
			return MembershipMetaData.PREFIX["0002"]
		}else if (prefixCode == "0003"){
			return MembershipMetaData.PREFIX["0003"]
		}else if (prefixCode == "0004"){
			return MembershipMetaData.PREFIX["0004"]
		}else if (prefixCode == "Z005"){
			return MembershipMetaData.PREFIX["Z005"]
		}else if (prefixCode == "Z001"){
			return MembershipMetaData.PREFIX["Z001"]
		}
		return prefixCode;
	},
	getHumanReadableSuffix : function(suffixCode){
		if (suffixCode == "0001"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["0001"]
		}else if (suffixCode == "0002"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["0002"]
		}else if (suffixCode == "0003"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["0003"]
		}else if (suffixCode == "0004"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["0004"]
		}else if (suffixCode == "0005"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["0005"]
		}else if (suffixCode == "0006"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["0006"]
		}else if (suffixCode == "0007"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["0007"]
		}else if (suffixCode == "Z001"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["Z001"]
		}else if (suffixCode == "Z002"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["Z002"]
		}else if (suffixCode == "Z003"){
			return MembershipMetaData.SUFFIX["Z003"]
		}
		return suffixCode;
	},
	unProtectFields : function(jqSelector){
		var formFields = $(jqSelector).find("input[type='text']  ,select");
		
		for (var i = 0; i < formFields.length; ++i) {
			var protect = $(formFields[i]).data("membership-widget-protect-field");
			
			if (MembershipMetaData.FIELD_TYPE.READ_ONLY != protect){
				if( $(formFields[i]).is('input')){
					$(formFields[i]).attr('readonly', false);
					$(formFields[i]).css({border: "1px solid #dbdbdb"});
				}else{
					$(formFields[i]).attr('disabled', false);
				}
				if(MembershipMetaData.FIELD_TYPE.EDITABLE_REQUIRED == protect){
					//$(formFields[i]).rules('add', { required:true});
					
				}else if (MembershipMetaData.FIELD_TYPE.DO_NOT_DISPLAY == protect){
					$(formFields[i]).val('');
					if( $(formFields[i]).is('input')){
						$(formFields[i]).attr('readonly', true);
						$(formFields[i]).css({border: "none"});
					}else{
						$(formFields[i]).attr('disabled', true);			
					}
				}	
			}
		}
	},
	protectFields : function(jqSelector){
		var formFields = $(jqSelector).find("input[type='text']  ,select");
		for (var i = 0; i < formFields.length; ++i) {
			if( $(formFields[i]).is('input')){
				$(formFields[i]).attr('readonly', true);
				$(formFields[i]).css({border: "none"});
			}else{
				$(formFields[i]).attr('disabled', true);			
			}
		}
	},
	protectDisplayFields : function(jqSelector){
		for (var i = 0; i < jqSelector.length; ++i) {
			var protection = $(jqSelector[i]).data('membership-widget-protect-field');	
    		if (MembershipMetaData.FIELD_TYPE.DO_NOT_DISPLAY == protection){
    			$(jqSelector[i]).hide();
    		}else{
    			$(jqSelector[i]).show();
    		}
		}
	},
	ajaxSend : function(){
		var spinner = '<div class="ui-widget-overlay ui-front r1_spinner" id="crmMetaDataGlobalSpinner"></div>'
		$("body").append( spinner );
	},
	ajaxComplete : function(){
		$('#crmMetaDataGlobalSpinner').remove();
	}
}

// Changing document.ready to window.onload, document.ready not workingin some pages for some reason
$(window).load(function(){
	
			if(typeof skipFooterMembershipMetaDataCall == 'undefined' || skipFooterMembershipMetaDataCall == false){
				var mosInfo = COSTCO.util.getMemberCookie();
				MembershipMetaData.getDataUrl = "https://" + location.hostname + "/AjaxCitiMembershipMetaDataView?langId=-24&storeId=10302&catalogId=11201";
				if($.cookie("capp_json") == null && mosInfo && mosInfo.signedIn == true && mosInfo.costcoMember == true){
					MembershipMetaData.ajaxHandler(MembershipMetaData.getDataUrl, null);
				}
			}
		
});
</script>

			<span class="bold">Why is this item marked as FSA Eligible?</span><br>This item is marked with the following icon as FSA eligible to identify that it MAY be purchased using a Flexible Spending Account (FSA):
		</p>
			<span class="fsa-link">FSA Eligible Item</span>
		<p>
			<span class="bold">What is a Flexible Spending Account (FSA)?</span><br>A FSA (Flexible Spending Account) allows use of the funds an individual has designated to be set aside pre-tax for medical expenses, typically with their employer, when selecting healthcare programs during the previous year.
		</p>
		<p>
			<span class="bold">What types of purchases are FSA eligible?</span><br>Over-the-counter medical supplies and equipment are considered reimbursable by an FSA account in 2011 and include the following categories:
		</p>
		<ul>
			<li>Contact lens solution</li>
			<li>Prescription contact lenses with correction only</li>
			<li>Diagnostic devices (i.e. blood pressure and blood glucose monitors)</li>
			<li>Durable medical equipment and goods</li>
			<li>Insulin</li>
			<li>Prescription medications</li>
		</ul>
		<p>
			<span class="bold italic">Note:</span> Although the IRS sets guidelines for FSA programs, <span class="italic">individual employers have the final determination of which expenses are covered by their FSA programs.</span>
		</p>
	</div>

	var shippingCountries = ['CA'];
	var billingCountries = ['CA','US'];
	var cookiesDisabledUrl = 'https://www.costco.ca/cookies-disabled.html';
	
	if (typeof checkCookieEnablement === "undefined") {
		function isCookieSupported() {
			var persist= true;
			do {
				var rand = Math.floor(Math.random()*100000000);
				var c= 'gCStest='+rand;
				document.cookie= persist? c+'; expires=Tue, 01-Jan-2030 00:00:00 GMT' : c;
				if (document.cookie.indexOf(c)!==-1) {
					document.cookie= c+'; expires=Sat, 01-Jan-2000 00:00:00 GMT';
					return persist;
				}
			} while (!(persist= !persist));
			return false;
		}
		
		function checkCookieEnablement() {
			if (!isCookieSupported() && window.location.href.indexOf('cookies-disabled') < 0) {
				window.location.replace(cookiesDisabledUrl);
			}
		};
	}
	
	checkCookieEnablement();

		<script>
		
		var initZoomViewer = function() {
			
			//returns zoom viewer size for the current window width
			function getViewerSize() {
				var width = $(window).width();
				if (width > 1000 || (width <= 667 && width > 382)) return zoomViewer.xl;
				if (width > 764) return zoomViewer.lg;
				return zoomViewer.xs;
			}
			
			//adds src attribute to script tag for the Rich Media zoom viewer library
			//and to img tag for the zoom viewer object to initiate injection by Rich Media
			function createViewer(viewerSize) {
				currentViewer = viewerSize;
				$viewerLib.attr('src', zoomViewer.libraryUrl + viewerSize);
				$viewerImg.attr('src', zoomViewer.viewerUrl + viewerSize.substr(2));
			}
			
			//changes size of viewer if current window size requires a different size
			function updateViewer() {
				var newViewerSize = getViewerSize();
				if (newViewerSize != currentViewer) {
					COSTCO.Global.logger('Window resized to new view. Updating zoomViewer');
					$viewerDiv.css('visibility', 'hidden');
					$initialImage.show();
					destroyThumbnailCarousel();
					RICHFX.load.fullReset();
					$viewerImg = $('#productImage');
					createViewer(newViewerSize);
					RICHFX.settings.init();
				}
				else if ($theViews.children().length) {
					adjustThumbnails();
				}
			}
			
			//adjusts thumbnail width and position of video overlay images
			function adjustThumbnails() {
				var thumbWidth = Math.floor($theViews.width() / 6);
				$theViews.find('img').css('width', thumbWidth);
				var $vidOverlay = $('img[id*=videoOverlay]');
				$vidOverlay.each(function() {
					$(this).parent().css('width', '');
					$(this).parent().css('height', '');
					$(this).css('left', $(this).siblings().position().left);
				});
			}
			
			//adds responsive properties to the zoom viewer
			function makeViewerResponsive() {
				COSTCO.Global.logger('richmedia.state.loaded - ZoomViewer injected. Adding responsive properties.');
				var $container = $('.RICHFXViewerContainer');
				$container.css('width', '');
				$container.css('height', '');
				$('#zoomViewer').find('img').addClass('img-responsive');
				if ($theViews.find('img').length) {
					$thumbnails.show();
					setupThumbnailCarousel();
				}
			}
			
			//creates thumbnail carousel
			function setupThumbnailCarousel(){
				if (currentSlide == 'undefined') {
					currentSlide = 0;
				}
				if (firstActiveSlide == 'undefined') {
					firstActiveSlide = 0;
				}
				var slides = $theViews.find('a').length;
				COSTCO.util.carousel($theViews,{
			        dots: false,
			        arrows: true,
			        slidesToShow: 5,
			        infinite: false,
			        slidesToScroll: 5,
			        autoplay: false,
			        draggable: true,
			        prevArrow: $('#viewsPrevArrow'),
			        nextArrow: $('#viewsNextArrow')
			    });
				$theViews.slick('slickGoTo', 5 * (Math.ceil(firstActiveSlide / 5)), true); //go to the set of 5 slides that were active
				$theViews.find('.selectedSlide').removeClass('selectedSlide');
				$theViews.find('.slick-slide:nth-child(' + (currentSlide + 1) + ')').addClass('selectedSlide');
				adjustThumbnails();
				if (slides > 5) {
					$prevArrow.addClass('slick-prev').css('visibility', 'visible');
					$nextArrow.addClass('slick-next').css('visibility', 'visible');
				}
				else {
					$prevArrow.css('visibility', 'hidden');
					$nextArrow.css('visibility', 'hidden');
				}
				$theViews.unbind('afterChange').on('afterChange', function() {
					firstActiveSlide = $('.slick-active').first().attr('data-slick-index');
				})
			}
			
			//destroys thumbnail carousel
			function destroyThumbnailCarousel() {
				$theViews.slick('destroy');
				$theViews.find('a[tabindex]').remove();
				$prevArrow.css('visibility', 'hidden');
				$prevArrow.css('visibility', 'hidden');
			}
			
			function loadVideoData() {
				COSTCO.Global.logger('External Video Detected. Loading Liveclicker.');
				$('#liveClickerCss').attr('href', zoomViewer.videoCssUrl);
				$.cachedScript(zoomViewer.videoJqueryUrl).done(function() {
					$.cachedScript(zoomViewer.videoJsUrl);
				});
				document.addEventListener('RichMedia.ExternalVideo.Show', function() {
					$('#zoomInstruction').hide();
				});
				document.addEventListener('RichMedia.ExternalVideo.Hide', function() {
					$('#zoomInstruction').show();
				})
			}
			
			var $viewerDiv = $('#zoomViewer');
			var $viewerLib = $('#productImageLibrary');
			var $viewerImg = $('#productImage');
			var $thumbnails = $('#thumbnails');
			var $theViews = $('#theViews');
			var $theSwatches = $('#theSwatches');
			var $initialImage = $('#initialProductImage');
			var $prevArrow = $('#viewsPrevArrow');
			var $nextArrow = $('#viewsNextArrow')
			var viewerSize = getViewerSize();
			var currentViewer = viewerSize;
			var currentSlide = 0;
			var firstActiveSlide = 0;
			
			document.addEventListener('richmedia.state.loaded', function() {
				makeViewerResponsive();
				if ($('.swatchDropdown').length > 0) { //select initial swatch
					try{
						var swatch = $('.swatchDropdown').find('option[data-swatch]').first().data('swatch');
						COSTCO.CMath.triggerSwatchDropDownSelection(swatch);
					}catch(e){
						console.log('error on loading inventoried swatch - default to first available');
						$theSwatches.find('img').first().click();
					}
				}
				$initialImage.hide();
				$viewerDiv.css('visibility', 'visible');
				var $externalVideo = $theViews.find('img[id*=External]');
				if (typeof lc == 'undefined' && $externalVideo.length > 0) { //only load liveclicker files once
					loadVideoData();
				}
			});
			document.addEventListener('richmedia.view.changed', function() {
				var $selected = $('.RICHFXColorChangeViewSelected');
				destroyThumbnailCarousel();
				currentSlide = $selected.parent().index();
				setupThumbnailCarousel();
			});
			document.addEventListener('richmedia.swatch.changed', function() {
				if ($theViews.hasClass('slick-initialized')) {
					destroyThumbnailCarousel();
					currentSlide = 0;
					firstActiveSlide = 0;
					setupThumbnailCarousel();
				}
			});
			createViewer(viewerSize);
			
			//modify viewer size on window resize
			$(window).resize(COSTCO.util.debounce(updateViewer, 250));
			
		}
		
		initZoomViewer();
		
		
</script>
		
		<div id="product-details" class="col-xs-12 col-sm-12 col-md-6 col-xl-5 pull-right">
			<div class="row visible-xl">
				<div class="col-xs-12"> 
					<div class="product-h1-container visible-xl-block">
					</div>
					
						<div id="details-bazaar-voice" class="bazaar-voice">
						</div>
					
						<p class='item-number'>Item #<span data-sku="483778" itemprop="sku">483778</span></p>
						
				</div>
			</div>
			<!-- Math table  -->
<div class="row form-group">
	<div class="col-xs-12 col-sm-12 col-xl-9">
	
<div id="math-table">
	<div id="breakdown" class="hide row no-gutter">
		
					
					<div class="online-price hide" data-opvalue="MjkuOTk=" data-catentry="880404" data-inv="IN_STOCK">
						<span class="op-label">Online Price</span>
						<span class="op-value">MjkuOTk=</span>

					</div>
